Special Education News

Research Report on Children's Life Guidance Group of Jiangsu Provincial Experimental Primary School Joint Association (II) 149

B. Taking Autonomy as an Extracurricular Activity Many people believe that children's activities can be divided into two types: in-class and extracurricular. In-class activities take teaching materials as the center, and extracurricular activities take undertakings as the center. In short, children's autonomy regards activities outside the classroom.

In fact, children's activities are whole, without in-class or extracurricular. Why do teachers have to forcibly divide children's whole activities into in-class and extracurricular with logical minds and adult eyes? For example, the activity of children's autumn outing, the collection of prohibited books, the sketches drawn, the diaries recorded, the travel notes written, many of these activities are done outside, some are done in school. How can this straight-line activity be divided into in-class and extracurricular?

C. Children's Autonomy is Preparing for the Future We cannot pre-determine many models based on social goals with adult minds and logical eyes, and produce them in the same way in factory-style schools. It is a pity that under this model-style training, I don't know how many lively children have been sacrificed, and I don't know how many small friends with rich personalities have been maimed.

(2) Organizational Morbidity

A. The Actual Aspect is Too Heavy and Superficial. When Children are a Kind of School Decoration No matter when you enter, no matter which school, you can definitely see some arrangements and the smell of children's autonomy. There are meetings and villages in the name, and you can hear them. In terms of arrangement, there must be several forms and signs about children's autonomy to see. In terms of activities, there must be patrolmen who seem to be on duty but are not, and farces of chaos can be encountered at their posts.

If you are interested and stand for a moment longer, you will definitely see many contrived autonomous activities appearing in your eyes.

If you are interested in asking the authorities about children's autonomy, you will definitely hear unexpected, lofty and great plans and policies vibrating in your eardrums.

B. In terms of Arrangement, Each School Organization, Everyone Should be Thorough and Complete, Neat and Consistent. However, the more complete the autonomous organization, the more it commits the problem of logicalization, and the more neat it is, the more it commits the drawback of mechanization. Therefore, the current general organization has two major problems in terms of arrangement: mechanization and logicalization.

(3) Morbidity in Implementation

A. Forgetting That Autonomy is Based on Children, Recognizing That the Object of Autonomy is Moral Education, Forgetting Children, So All Autonomous Facilities, Organizations, and Guidance Cannot Be Based on Children, Placing Children in a Passive Position, So Many Activities are Mechanized. Activities are Lively, Children are Children Themselves Although there are activities, the children themselves are also at a loss.

D. Not Based on [Children's Needs | Children's Autonomy Each activity must be based on children's needs, then that kind of activity is valuable. However, most schools, in order to make the autonomous organization complete and thorough, disregard children's needs, stipulate various activities, formulate detailed regulations, plan various methods, and then ask children to participate in the activities. May I ask how much educational value this kind of activity has?

(3) Theoretical Basis of Children's Life Guidance

Education is Life, Life is Education We should declare the death penalty for this kind of children's autonomy that is full of morbidity. At the very least, we also hope that he will have a little (die a natural death).

We advocate making children follow their lives and achieve their own achievements. We do not advocate using means to teach children, nor do we want to use magic to drive children.

We want to discover some meeting goals in children's whole activities and are unwilling to prepare meeting goals and take children to create an ideal type for one person or several people.

We only know that education is life and life is education. In order to achieve this goal, we try our best to delve into the center of children's activities and strive for the development of children's lives.

Now, we will make a profound review of the meaning and scope of life and make an accurate analysis of human life. Under this review and analysis, we can see the source of children's life guidance.

However, we will further explain in detail the methods of life guidance, and carefully establish the goals of life guidance. Under the explanation and establishment of these methods and goals, we can see the guide for life guidance activities.

(1) The Meaning of Life Guidance || In the current educational field, life and education are in a state of separation, and the entire education feels that it has lost its vitality. Therefore, education and life should be combined. Education occupies the entire life, so the entire education has the meaning of life.

Education takes life as its object. Life guidance is to make children's current life develop upwards infinitely. Therefore, life should not be separated from education, and education cannot be separated from life.

The current morbid children's autonomous activities are far from life, and life cannot be the center of activities. No wonder children's autonomy is full of mechanical meaning.

(2) The Scope of Life Guidance || The object of the scope of life can be in the entire life, and its content also includes the entire life of human life. In terms of time, there is a trinity of past, present, and future life. In terms of space, there is a trinity relationship of family, school, and society. Children's past life is the family, the present life is the school, and the future life is the society. Therefore, in children's entire life activities, the scope of life guidance should be linked to the past family life, enrich the current school life, and develop the future social life. But the current school is separated from the family and separated from society. How can this kind of unfounded and unrealistic education be called vitality?

(3) Analysis of Human Life Activities in Life Guidance || We will first study the human life based on the modern educationists' method of summarizing human life activities for reference. The contemporary experts who study courses take Babbitt, Sun Shihui, and Ban Lolan as the leaders. They summarize the methods of human life as follows:

(A) Babbitt Summarizes Human Life Activities into Five Aspects:

(1) Language Activities

(2) Occupational Activities

(3) Health Activities

(4) Civic Activities

(5) Leisure Activities

Babbitt's meaning is that language occupies a very important position in the entire life, so it is summarized as a major human activity.

In fact, in the entire life of the school, there are many opportunities for language activities, and language can be learned at any time in various activities.

Important News

Fully Develop Beiping Culture in the Most Economical Way 150

Guidance Committee Hopes to be Established in January or February

Li Shizeng's Speech in Beiping

Beiping Correspondence Central Committee Member Li Shizeng went to live in Xishan after arriving in Beiping. He returned to Beiping at 11:00 AM yesterday (the 22nd). At 5:00 PM in the afternoon, he invited the education and news circles to a tea party at the Beiping Research Conference Room, with more than 20 people attending. Mr. Quan gave a speech as follows:

I am very happy that everyone has come to gather and talk today, and I am also very sorry. After arriving in Beiping, my brother stayed in Xishan for a few days due to fatigue along the way. Some of you have come to visit once or twice. I wanted to visit each of you, but I did not have enough time. Because someone wrote a letter wanting to have a meeting in a short period of time, I invited friends from the news and education circles to talk at the same time today. It is not a tea party to entertain the news media or various circles in general. Friends came to visit, more or less, with a visiting nature, asking about my mission and opinions this time. Many people in Tianjin have asked about this. My brother has no special mission to Beiping this time. I am deeply grateful and uneasy for your welcome. My brother has lived in Beiping for a long time, and Beiping is my second hometown. I often travel back and forth between Beijing and Beiping. I have no special mission, so I should not be welcomed. My brother travels between Beijing and other places. Except for the obstruction of traffic due to the war, I always travel back and forth once every one or two months. Although I have not seen you for eight months this time, it is no different from usual. There is really no problem. However, I am of course happy to meet with friends I have not seen for a long time. It is also because of this separation of eight or nine months that friends have come to inquire. Based on experience, the questions are all about a few things. First, I will give a general answer to the few things I have thought of. If there are any questions later, I will answer them separately.

Regarding the matter of the Guidance Committee for Reorganizing Beiping Culture, I have already answered in Tianjin. Today, I will restate or supplement one point. Beiping is important in culture, which is universally recognized. Everyone has already paid attention to this. In recent times, it can be divided into two items: one is a purely cultural issue, and the other is an issue related to the current situation. There are also issues related to the economy, so it can also be divided into three points. Beiping culture has long been noticed by the general public. For example, paying attention to the preservation of the Forbidden City and other general antiques is one example. About a year ago, Mr. Zhang Puquan, a member of the Preservation Committee of the Palace Museum, suggested to the Central Government to set up a general agency for the preservation of antiques in Beiping. At that time, the Central Government handed it over to Mr. Ye Chucong and my brother for review. Later, because he left Beijing, he did not have time to review it. Half a year ago, Mr. Wu Zhihui proposed to change Beiping into a cultural district because Beiping was the old imperial capital and was easy to seize the opportunity with the reorganization faction as the political center to make it a cultural center reform. At that time, it was fighting, and the Central Government expressed sympathy for this proposal. Because it was about the north, it specifically sought the opinion of Deputy Commander Zhang, who also extremely agreed. At the Fourth Plenary Session, Mr. He Xuechu had a proposal to prosper Beiping. Because the resolution was to review the case together, this case was established. Because Mr. Wu Zhihui, He Xuechu, Ye Chucong, Zhang Puquan, and my brother et al. had a review relationship, it was proposed to set up a guidance committee for reorganizing Beijing culture. Therefore, the former was purely related to culture, and the latter was also related to the current situation. However, since the reorganization faction government collapsed, Beiping has naturally lost its qualifications as a political center and has become a cultural center. However, after the capital moved south, the economy has declined day by day. Now that the provincial government has moved to Tianjin, it is even worse. If we want to preserve the culture, we must also seek economic development. In other words, we will use economic methods to maintain and develop it to become a cultural center. The culture mentioned here is a broad sense of culture, not only referring to education and academics, but also including industry and crafts. Whether Beiping can become a large industrial area in the future, I dare not say at this time. However, the original handicrafts really need to be preserved and promoted. Mr. Wu Zhihui once proposed to actively develop wool fabrics in Beiping, which is one aspect. Therefore, in summary, the guidance committee for reorganizing Beiping culture really has the above-mentioned three relationships: culture, economy, and current situation. This is the entire initiation and process. I hope that the meeting will be established within one or two months, led by the Central Government, to provide a strong and powerful assistance to prosper Beiping. The local government will work together to make progress and make Beiping change into a new atmosphere. And I firmly believe that this hope will be fully achieved. (To be continued)

It was found that the school principal Tang Guoxun did not investigate in depth after the teacher Zhang Xiuxiong took students Tang Jingen, etc. to Zhoupu to compete in basketball on October 4th of this year, which led to the occurrence of the conspiracy and fraud on October 18th. Although the school principal was on sick leave at the time, he could not avoid the blame for negligence. Lu Yiyan Creates Three Kinds of Character Search Methods 154

When Lu Yiyan was editing the dictionary at the Zhonghua Book Company in the Republic of China's 10s, he began to study character search methods. As a result of the research, there are five types. The first achievement is the (Head and Tail Number Character Search Method). This method divides the strokes into ten categories and represents them with numbers. The first two strokes and the last two strokes of each character are compiled into numbers, which is extremely convenient for checking. The New National Pronunciation Student Dictionary compiled with the head and tail numbers has been published by the Zhonghua Book Company and has been popular throughout the country. The third type (Head Character Search Method) This method follows the structure of the characters, counts the head characters and side characters, and divides them into 132 parts. The character positions in each part also use the most popular and simple methods to fix and improve the standard of the radicals. A small dictionary of national pronunciation has been printed by the Zhonghua Book Company and will be published next spring. The third type is (Up and Down Number Character Search Method) This method divides the strokes into nine categories and represents them with numbers. The top two strokes and the bottom two strokes of each character are compiled into numbers. The method is novel and the check is convenient. Now, a book of character strokes has been compiled and has been typeset and will be published next year.

White Goose Painting Research Institute Registered 155

The famous art organization, the White Goose Painting Research Institute, was originally founded by painters Chen Qiucao, Gu Xuelu, etc. Established for two years, it has enjoyed high reputation, has strict purposes, beautiful facilities, and its organizational discipline is particularly rare in the domestic art world. Recently, the institute has been approved for registration by the Special City Party Department and the Bureau of Education, obtaining Permit No. 11 from the City Party Department and Registration Certificate No. 17 from the Bureau of Education. It has also been submitted to the Municipal Government and the Ministry of Education for record. It plans to expand its organization starting next spring and implement new plans. Therefore, the research period of this session will be terminated earlier than usual for the general New Year holiday to allow for a longer period of consideration for construction matters, so that it can be more perfect.

Zhenru Eliminates the Navy 160

Three to Zero, Zhenru Wins

Senior Cup Two-Week Tournament

The Zhenru Football Team played a Senior Cup two-week tournament with the British Navy yesterday afternoon at the Chinese Baseball Field. As a result, Zhenru won three to zero, and the British Navy was eliminated. Three to four thousand spectators watched the game, which was a great event.

(1) A Glimpse of the Two Teams' Formations

Zhenru's lineup yesterday was the best for the team. The British Navy was almost the same as the one against Lehua the day before, so the outcome was expected. It was just a matter of the score. In the first half, Zhenru was triumphant and controlled everything. The Navy was seen scurrying around. In the second half, the formation changed, and the Navy also frequently invaded. The enemy's traces almost shook the goal, but the clowns jumping around did not achieve anything. Zhenru also did not achieve much. Therefore, the score in the first half determined the outcome. The Zhenru team performed well overall, but not as well in the second half as in the first half. The lineups of the two teams are listed below:

Zhenru Team

Liang Guanlian Feng Yunyou Jiang Shanjing Lin Songfa Chen Zhenhe Zhuang Shihong

Chen Bingxiang Luo Guanghai Dai Linjing Chen Jiaqiu Mei Hongbao

British Navy

Haimen Smith Cox Ashmon Robertson Hinston

Gore Crawford Huiai Tuole Xu Nadingge

(2) Zhenru Scores Three Goals in a Row

After fifteen minutes of melee, the referee Maxwell blew the whistle. The British Navy kicked off. After one or two circles, Luo Haiguang took the ball away but was intercepted. Suddenly, the forward lost his footing, and the Navy attacked twice, but both times it was calm. Zhenru also attacked repeatedly but failed. Mei Hongbao shot but missed. Chen Bingxiang failed to catch the ball. After fifteen minutes of melee, the situation suddenly changed. When everyone was bored, Chen Zhongjian came from afar and kicked the ball. Center forward Dai bumped forward and picked it up. The Navy goalkeeper Haimen pushed it up, and Luo Haiguang headed it in. The ball was in the net. With one goal scored, everyone cheered and their spirits were lifted.

With the way open, the momentum surged. The Zhenru players attacked the enemy and scored another goal, but it was disallowed due to offside. After waiting five more minutes, the ball came from Luo to Mei Hongbao, who passed it forward. Chen Jiaqiu, with his swift feet, went straight in and Haimen had to wait for his death, resulting in a score of two to zero. In less than two minutes, Chen Zhenhe passed to center forward Dai, who sent it to the right wing. Mei Hongbao accurately made it three to zero. The first half ended like this.

(3) The Navy Sighs at the Goal

Suddenly, at the start of the second half, the situation changed, Zhenru failed to attack, and instead frequently received empty scares from the Navy. Dangerous situations were often seen. It was almost the Navy's last stand. The Navy had no less than ten chances to attack the goal. However, they lightly sent the opportunities away and the shot was either inaccurate or flew over the goal. If the shot had been accurate, the situation would have changed dramatically. After forty-five minutes of melee, nothing was gained and the game ended.

The offside restricts the five forwards, and some may wonder about the different situations of Zhenru in the upper and lower halves. First, they charged in one breath and then weakened slightly. Second, they had already won three goals and were sure of the victory, so their fighting spirit was relaxed. The most important thing was that the referee's offside whistle blew continuously, startling the Zhenru five forwards so that they dared not enter the line, and they were too cautious, so they did not achieve anything in the second half. This was the main reason.

Free Talk: Ke Copper

Laugh It Off · Seafarer 181

Man (Waiting for his lover on the street corner. Having strained his eyes and stood on his legs until they ached.) Why is she always late? Has she forgotten about me?

Woman (After an unknown amount of time, she finally arrives leisurely.) Were you waiting for me?

Man (Forcing a gentle tone) My love, you seem to be a little late.

Woman Only a few minutes late. What's the big deal?

Man (Surprised) Only a few minutes?

Woman I said I would be here at seven o'clock. It's only twenty minutes past now. (Looking at her wristwatch)

Man In that case, you must have mistaken the date. I have been waiting since seven o'clock last night until now.

Mother (Asking her eight-year-old son) I told you to sleep well. Why did you run out again?

Son I still have something to do. I want to see Father.

Mother What else do you have to do?

Son Didn't Mother tell me (that one should always be kind, and if anyone bullies you, you should forgive them, so that you can sleep well at night)? Tonight, Father beat me and wouldn't let me eat oranges. He has bullied me enough. When I was sleeping, I remembered Mother's words, so I specially ran out to forgive him.

Housewife (Asking the milkman) How much do we owe you?

Milkman Madam, let me calculate for a moment. (Calculating with his fingers while there is the sound of a woman singing in the room)

Housewife (Shouting loudly to her daughter) Aju, stop singing for a moment. The milkman is calculating the bill here.

Milkman Madam, it's okay. Fortunately, I'm used to hearing the yellow cattle calling.

Prediction of World War II · Homeless 182

General Erich Ludendorff of Germany, in his new book, says that based on the current military situation of European countries and scientific calculations, World War II will definitely begin on May 1, 1932. It will start with a conflict between Italy and France and spread throughout Europe. Germany will be the battlefield. After the book was published, some people scoffed at it as nonsense, but many believed that Ludendorff was a key figure in the European War and must have research value. The following is a translation of the main points:

The Course of the War France will unite with Poland, Belgium, Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, Romania, and other countries, with a total of about 12 million people. Italy will unite with Germany, Austria, and England, but the number of people will only be about 18 million. The war will last about six weeks. France and Poland will win a great victory. On the first night of the war, the bombers of France, Poland, Czechoslovakia, and other countries will destroy all the most important cities in Germany. Austria and other countries will also be ravaged by France and Poland, and the Tyrol area will be occupied and a military government will be established. France and Italy will join forces on the plains of southern Germany. The most important Ruhr area in Germany will be occupied by the French army eight days after the start of the war. The German government will move to Kiel, where British troops will land to command the military affairs of northern Germany, which may avoid the trampling of the French army. In the fifth week after the start of the war, the French and Italian armies will determine the outcome.

The War After the War Although France and Poland are victorious countries, they will not be able to enjoy the blessings of victory. Because the Soviet Russia is lurking behind, it will raise a large army. The number of people will be between 600 and 700 million, and there will be 100 million Turkish troops to help. Poland and Romania will bear the brunt. From the Baltic Sea to the Adriatic Sea, France and Russia will begin to fight. At this time, the people will suffer greatly from the war and will definitely rise up in revolution. The United States will also be affected by the European war, and wars will occur repeatedly. The whole world will be reduced to a barbaric area.

Suzhou Park Goldfish Exhibition · Zhi Wei 183

The goldfish exhibition is a creation that has never been seen in thousands of years. It is said that the motive for launching this exhibition was that Suzhou Park added 30 to 40 display tanks this year. The park staff member Wu Ziji personally supervised the fish farmers to take good care of the fish. The fish have become fat and have unique characteristics. So Mr. Fan Yunshu, the director of the park, discussed with Mr. Wu Guanghan, the director of the Education Bureau, and went out to solicit famous species and prepare for half a month, borrowing glass tanks and arranging the locations, which took a lot of effort. Unfortunately, it rained all day on the originally scheduled 20th and 21st, and tourists were reluctant to come. Fortunately, the third day was sunny. From morning to night, tourists gathered, reaching thousands of people. For a time, shoulders rubbed against each other, and there was almost no place to set foot in the East Studio and West Pavilion. It can be said to be extremely grand. The (upturned gills silver egg) (red and white dragon species pompon) of the Sun family of Sijing Lane are indeed extraordinary. Unfortunately, they belong to young fish like Bao Jiemi. Other details are not described. Please forgive me. I think the second goldfish exhibition will have more to watch. Please wait and see.

Travels in Southeast Asia (113) 185

Burmese customs have a water-splashing ceremony when the rainy season is about to arrive (around March 15 of the lunar calendar). Water is splashed for three days. When the rainy season is about to end (around September 15 of the lunar calendar), a fire-lighting ceremony is held. Each household hangs candles for three days to mark it. These are the two major ceremonies of the year. After the rainy season ends, it never rains again until the following year. The climate is dry and warm, which is considered winter. However, after the dry and warm season, around February and March of the lunar calendar, it is summer. The heat is abnormal, which people find to be bitter. After summer comes the rainy season.

The terrain in northern Burma is mountainous. The mountains bordering Yunnan are the source of the rivers. Therefore, minerals are produced. The rivers are turbulent and not conducive to navigation. The central part has many fields. To the southern downstream, there are very few mountains, and it is entirely a swamp. Water transportation is very good. The water is deep and the waves are calm. Even small rivers are very deep, which is beneficial to wheel boats. However, the water level rises and falls regularly, unlike China's abnormal heights and lows. Therefore, the residents' thatched houses are mostly located near the waterfront, built on the water, to enjoy the convenience of bathing without the danger of being washed away. Men, women, and children are all good at swimming. When the sun sets in the west, the river is full of pairs of swimming fish, and men and women come to bathe. This is the most enjoyable time for the Burmese.

Commercial power is controlled by women. Women are all able to read and calculate. They are diligent, clean, and love beauty. Therefore, it must be known that Burmese customs value women and despise men. This is because women are the center of ethics. Women have an obligation to be filial to their families and parents. Many men marry into their families. Therefore, marrying a Burmese woman requires assuming the obligations of her entire family. This must be known. The reason why they despise men is that men grow up and either become monks and leave home, or marry into other families and leave. They cannot support their parents or support the family. Therefore, they are despised. This custom is exactly the opposite of China's. Although this is not the world I advocate, where women transform and become equal, the submission of the male can be said to be very small in Burma. And after a man enters the woman's family, he enjoys the right to divide the property. If the woman's family has property, the man can also enjoy it. It's like a middleman marrying a woman. Alas. Love is the root of suicide.

A thousand sails pass by the side of the sunken ship. Why criticize the plane for aviation carelessness? Ten thousand trees bloom in front of the dead tree. Just shade for future generations, and plant good trees by hand.

See through everything, there has never been a hundred-year-old person in a hundred years. Be careful in everything, there are stronger hands among the strong.

Splitting thunder hits tofu. Obviously, it is choosing the soft one to deceive the old man. Longevity star swallows arsenic, living for a long time is looking for a way to die.

Without three points of autocracy, one cannot govern a family, let alone a country. If you are sincere, you can move even different species, let alone people of the same kind.

There is a way to please everyone. There is no policy that pleases everyone. There is a war that wins every battle, but there is no army that never loses.

Electrification is advancing with each passing day, resulting in unprecedented strange devices. Knowledge is evolving, and saints combining Chinese and Western cultures will be produced.

It is difficult to stop the horse on a precipice. There must be a method that must be carried out. Teaching monkeys to climb trees. Beware of people who reward evil.

Great kindness is not repaid. Peng and Han cannot be killed. Heavy trust is not returned. Cao and Mang cannot be written.

The gentleman of heaven, the villain of man. Turn it around, the villain of heaven, the gentleman of man. The ancient sage, the present corrupt. Turn it over, the ancient corrupt, the present sage.

Thousand-mile eye, downwind ear. Human nature is full of wonders. The eyes can see, the ears can hear. I feel that there is nothing that is not strange.

Six thieves, six senses, six dusts. The most distressing thing is to be employed by the form. One day, one month, one year. The most painful thing is that time will not come again.

No wind, no waves. Noise is the tide. If the steps can ascend to heaven. Fighting starts from competition.

Holding a precious sword to kill flies. Foolishly moving the fire of ignorance. Swallowing arsenic to scare tigers. Leaving a book of last words in vain.

Sorrow for the exhaustion of vitality. Therefore, mountain apes and cranes will be transformed into worms and sand again. Be alarmed by the excessive number of doctrines. The new land dragon snakes are divided into colors.

It seems that the historical figures are nothing more than bandits and slaves of both sexes. Except for the celestial Buddhas in the sky, everything returns to eating, drinking, men, and women.

European Travelogue (92) · Liu Haisu 186

Pilgrimage to Italy Diary

(3) Ten Days in Rome (10) (5)

June 4, Day in Europe: Great Cathedral of St. Peter｜Vatican Palace｜Sistine Chapel｜

After lingering and sighing in this great cathedral for a long time, we walked through the colonnade to visit the Vatican Museum in the backyard. Before we arrived at the museum, we had a general look at the entire scale of the Royal Palace. The surrounding palaces and towering buildings were scorched by the Roman sun under the dry blue sky, shining with a rare golden yellow, and in every glittering place, the sacred majesty of religion was revealed. On the left and right of the palace gate, there were several layers of armed guards. These guards were too strange and cute. Everyone looked like the "Golden Leopard" performed on the Shanghai stage, wearing (red) (yellow) (green) various colors of mixed and different uniforms, and wearing a gold chain like a rosary between the legs wrapped in blue, red, and red cloth. Holding a long spear in his hand, the stem was painted in vermilion and the tip was bright silver. It looked very heroic and mighty. This is to tell us that the Pope is inviolable.

Walking along the Royal Palace for more than ten feet to the end, we stepped into the Vatican Museum. Immediately, I raised the deep taste of my research. This museum is different from other museums in Rome. The entrance fee is five lire per person. It is said that this is the Pope's income. In Rome, all places under the jurisdiction of the Pope require a fee.

After entering the door, we walked into the rectangular corridor. The visitors gathered and blocked the road. At this time, our hearts were only anxiously waiting. Especially me, I was really as happy as entering a treasure trove. This kind of interest is rarely seen in my life. Ascending the stone steps to become a broad corridor, the walls on the left and right and the ceiling are painted with brightly colored stories of the Virgin and Christ. It is a kind of glue painting fresco. The cabinets on both sides display the treasures used by the popes of the past. Foreign gifts, Egyptian handicrafts, many small wooden statues, and many decorative arts. Relief. Ivory carvings, etc. Most of these are things left by Egypt and Greece for thousands of years. I didn't have time to examine them one by one at this time. I only felt that in this unfolding new situation, every item was not surprising. There was also a room inside, which was also full of valuable items such as gold, silver, and jade. There were also many religious documents. The surrounding decorations were also extremely gorgeous. What was painted on the walls was neither heaven nor hell, but very lively animals (ducks) (doves) (peacocks). Or delicious grapes. From this, it can be known that the source of beauty has already turned from taking the grade to the fields and paying attention to observing nature. Especially surprising is that some frescoes are indeed very similar to the frescoes in ancient Chinese temples. The colors and brushstrokes also have the same flavor. However, it is not forced at all, but a very natural thing. This is surprising and strange.

Green Garden

A New Method of Teaching Children to Write, Sweeping the Land 187

The Nine Brush Methods of Zhuo Junyong

In the context of modern cultural development, the appreciation of calligraphy must also adopt a new perspective. Generally speaking, the writing of modern characters should prioritize simplicity and evenness as beauty, ease of writing as legitimacy, and the ability to incorporate the advantages of various styles as its utmost achievement. In other words, while in the past, only those with leisure and strength could write well, now everyone can be taught to write well.

The term "Chinese characters" does not necessarily refer to the commonly used regular script of recent times. Judging from current trends, a new type of script is bound to emerge to meet this demand. This script will inevitably be very simple, very even, easy to recognize, and easy to write. Those who are mindful of cultural undertakings must have already heard the call for this.

However, before this new script becomes widespread, there is still a need for an improved method of calligraphy to meet current needs. Why? It's not that the currently used regular script cannot produce good writing, but rather that it has been ruined by those who write in the (wuguangfang) style. The lack of attention to calligraphy has been most severe in recent decades. From the very beginning, when primary school students start copying models, they are copying the characters of contemporary officials, which are then carved by printing shops into extremely rigid and mediocre forms. No one can look at them without feeling nauseated. Imagine that those who are just learning to hold a brush start with such characters. Even if they later want to emulate the best, their habits have already formed, and how much further progress can they make? Therefore, starting off with an improper method of writing can be likened to a woman binding her feet from childhood. Once the feet have been bound, even if they are later unbound, walking will still be unnatural. Those who have written bad characters will find it difficult to get rid of their old bad habits. This is speaking for those who have aspirations to improve. If someone doesn't study calligraphy, they will never know their own shortcomings. The decline in Chinese people's handwriting can be seen in various public places. Just look at the street, and the large, resplendent characters of the shop signs and advertisements on both sides, no matter how ornate, are always in a poor and unappealing style. The result of this poor quality is that it fails to attract people's attention, fails to evoke a sense of beauty, and makes it difficult for people to recognize the characters. What a significant loss this is for business!

Japan shares the same writing system as China, but most Japanese people write better than we do. There is no other reason for this than that they have not had their feet bound and have not copied bad models. They start with cursive script, using brushwork close to the Tang dynasty models. This is not the best method, but the result is already much better than ours. The lack of attention to calligraphy not only results in losses in social applications but also poses a major problem in children's education. Think of how precious children's minds are. Other subjects have scientific teaching methods, allowing them to acquire the most complex knowledge in the simplest way. Only in writing Chinese characters do we still use the old, irregular methods, forcing rote learning. How unfortunate this is for children!

There is nothing that cannot be summarized using scientific methods. Therefore, it is not impossible to improve the teaching of calligraphy to promote its advancement. Recently, Mr. Zhuo Junyong created a "Nine Brush Methods," which arose in response to this demand. His basic method is to reduce the various complex brush techniques to the following nine: (1) Dot, (2) Horizontal, (3) Vertical, (4) Left Oblique, (5) Right Oblique, (6) Left Turn, (7) Right Turn, (8) Left Spiral, (9) Right Spiral. These nine brush strokes are all geometric shapes. If further reduced, there are actually only four types: (1) Dot Shape, (2) Line Shape, (3) Angle, (4) Circle. Beginners only need to use the brush to trace these four shapes, mastering them skillfully, and they will naturally be able to write well.

At first glance, his theory may seem too outlandish, but it is based on sound and irrefutable reasoning. You must understand that the reason why Chinese characters can be written well does not lie in the shape and structure of each individual character, but in the brushwork. If the brushwork is proper, the structure can be inferred and applied to other characters. Conversely, if the structure is good but the brushwork is improper, it still cannot produce good writing. Therefore, the foundation lies in brushwork. The traditionally transmitted "Eight Principles of Yong" have some merit, but they are too complex for beginners to grasp and are designed specifically for regular script, not suitable for modern, liberated styles. According to Zhuo himself, these nine methods can encompass the brushwork of various scripts, including oracle bone, seal script, clerical script, cursive script, regular script, and running script. After mastering these nine methods, one can write any of the above-mentioned scripts. This is indeed the special essence of this book.

If primary school students use this as a model, they can achieve at least the following results: (1) They will not rely on established styles and will not be bound by vulgar forms, which is most suitable for children's psychology; (2) The horizontal strokes will be flat and the vertical strokes straight, fostering good habits of hand-eye coordination; (3) They can gradually advance to higher levels and engage in seal script, clerical script, and cursive script.

Not only children but also ordinary people who aspire to study calligraphy can find a simple and easy path to entry. If they enter the door with the right method, they only need to copy one or two steles and rubbings, and they will not have to worry about being unable to write well. Otherwise, even if they practice every day, like the ancients who (darkened the pool with ink), it will still be in vain. I think few people have experienced this kind of suffering. Therefore, what is most needed today in promoting calligraphy is not necessarily good steles and rubbings, but rather a good and simple method of entry. Zhuo's book can indeed meet this need, and its success can be predicted.

Written to Bao Jun (Continued) by Cheng Bing 188

○○○

Because of this, I have thought of suicide several times. I thought, this love affair is unlikely to succeed, no matter what. I don't need to fantasize anymore. I should be brave and shoot myself with a gun. That's it, that's it.

But, Bao Jun, it's easy to say, but difficult to do. I don't know if I'm afraid of death, let's not talk about it for now. But, Bao Jun, you know that to shoot myself with a gun, where can I get a gun? I don't have one, so how can I shoot myself? Or I can talk about other ways to die, but, Bao Jun, since I can't love the person I want to love, then my death should be a grand and joyful one. As for hanging and drowning, those are just the actions of women and children. I am not worthy and unwilling to do them.

Moreover, I have another reason that I want to explain to you, which is that I really don't want to die, because I can't bear to give up loving her. Alas, Bao Jun, if she wants me to die, I am willing. If she wants me to be her faithful slave, I am willing. But now, she doesn't even give me a chance to talk to her. Without her attitude being clearly expressed, I can't commit suicide no matter what. I really can't bear to abandon her and commit suicide.

○○○○

I have a fellow villager, Wang Jun, who also knows about this. What he said to me is this: he thinks that I only have two options to take towards that LSUM, and there is no third way to go. One is to actively start an offensive against her, and the other is to absolutely give up this attempt. But, Bao Jun, I feel that both of these methods are impossible now. Giving up my love is better than shooting myself with a gun. Am I that kind of person? Can I give it up? If so, then my writing this letter to you is completely meaningless. That being said, then I should start an active offensive against her, but Bao Jun, I have already told you this before. If I were a courageous person, I'm afraid I would have already thrown myself into her arms. But me, me, Bao Jun, I am originally a coward. (To be continued)

Book and Newspaper Introductions

Fragrant Kiss by Xiaotian 189

Written by Zou Fang, published by Caoyehua

In the extremely silent Chinese poetry scene, we are able to read such a long lyric poem as "Fragrant Kiss," which truly makes us feel unexpectedly delighted. This is because recently, there have been hardly any individual collections of poetry published in bookstores. Even if one or two so-called collections of poetry emerge on the silent poetry scene like phoenix feathers and unicorn horns, there are very few that can make readers feel particularly satisfied. In fact, it can be said that there are none. This is truly a sign of the decline and lifelessness of the Chinese poetry scene. Those who love poetry are of course filled with endless sorrow. Although, not long ago, various publications paid attention to the selection of poems, most of them belonged to the category of slogans and labels, making us feel only their crudeness, horror, and bloody murderousness when we recited them. They had neither artistic expression nor technical expertise to speak of. These shouted-out poems simply forgot the essence and elements of poetry. This is a fact that everyone admits. The poems in this collection ("Fragrant Kiss") are greatly different. They express without reservation the passionate emotions, rich imagination, and the elements of simple beauty that a poem should have. At the same time, the author's technique has also reached a mature point, which is even more unattainable in the current general poetry. Regarding this, Mr. Fu Donghua writes in great detail in the preface to this collection, writing like this:

"If one were to take the pulse, as it were, and calmly and attentively press down on several poems in "Fragrant Kiss," one would feel that they contain intense emotions like smoldering fire. Such smoldering fire is precisely the quality of a poet, which others cannot force. When the technique of expression becomes more mature, this quality can be developed into the brilliant mark of art. Therefore, I have great hope for the author as a poet."

In this short preface, the special qualities of the poems in "Fragrant Kiss" are analyzed in an exceptionally detailed manner. If we then read the original poem (calmly and attentively), we will feel even more that Mr. Fu's words are extremely correct. However, we cannot deny that the author, as a poet, already possesses the necessary conditions.

Moreover, the author's thoughts are very lofty, which may be the thoughts of a poet. Therefore, in the expression of each verse, he makes every effort to use his artistic skill, not allowing it to fall into mediocrity, no matter what. This is not so novel and pleasing in the expressions of ordinary poets in general. Those who have read this ("Fragrant Kiss") will surely believe it. What the author writes has a strict order. The entire poem is divided into six kisses, and each kiss is further divided into several small sections, but it does not feel complicated at all. After we sing and recite it, we feel that what he writes is well-organized, which is extremely evident. What the author expresses is for the sake of love, but on the other hand, it is filled with an upward consciousness. This is the greatness of the author, which those decadent poets cannot express. Now let's first look at what he writes:

Your cheeks have never been, stained with rouge and white lead,

I love this smile, like a lily just unfolding its petals,

Regardless of what is rippling, whether it is tranquility or joy,

Ah, please, allow me to be frivolous again,

| Or, joy, or, tranquility, (Second Kiss)

Little girl, I love your innocence,

Who says children and adults are different?

(Children can enter the Kingdom of Heaven),

Have you ever heard someone say this? After all, God likes jealousy,

Love has been born, and fallen into sorrow,

I almost want to destroy myself,

Why not wait for me to think about it anew, (First Kiss),

From the two verses cited above, we can see that the author is optimistic. Since he is filled with (joy), the future of course contains unlimited hope. This is truly because the author has a lively and innocent air. He loves nature, and he loves innocent and bright little girls. This is none other than his love and protection of precious childhood, and his hope to strive upwards. This is a kind of symbolic brushstroke. Although he sometimes feels sorrow, he always wants to add a new assessment to these, returning to the new realm of childhood. In the following verses, what he writes about the love of (children) is even more vivid and delightful, but it is mostly filled with joy.

Pour a glass of wine | Drink as much as you can,

Liang, we haven't met for half a year, how rare is today,

I wish you happiness, I wish myself happiness,

East, west, north, south, all are filled with joy,

Joy, joy, joy

I congratulate myself, you celebrate my resurrection,

Joy, joy, joy (Fourth Kiss)

Like these two verses, what is expressed is how powerful, compact, and novel, making us feel endless joy in our lively hearts. This point is very worthy of attention. In general, this collection ("Fragrant Kiss") is a newly discovered lyric poem in the domestic poetry scene that is not easy to obtain. Regarding this, Mr. Zhao Jingshen has said it very clearly in his preface, so there is no need for me to explain it in detail. In my opinion, it is fully meaningful to recommend this ("Fragrant Kiss") poetry collection to readers.
